  • Syntax Highlighter

Syntax Highlighter

A syntax highlighter based on hljs.js library which support 192 languages out of the box. It can be used on Slides or Markdown cells:

.md

Let's highlight something

<HLJS Lang={"html"}>
<Escape>
<ul class="list">
  <li></li>
  <li></li>
  <li></li>
</ul>
</Escape>
</HLJS>

Source codeâ€‹

To embed this component into your workflow:

  1. Paste this text into an empty input cell

  1. Evaluate the Wolfram Language definitions for HLJS:
HLJS[code_, Rule["Lang", lang_String]] := CreateFrontEndObject[
  HLJSView[code // ToStringRiffle, lang]
]
